# Rug Bear Skin

# Description __

A decorative rug that can be placed on walls, floors, and ceilings. Provides comfort when in close proximity.

Page views: 3,477  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Rustige Egg - Red

# Description __

An exquisite hand crafted gold and diamond egg. When opened, a very special melody can be heard as you observe an intricate representation of your favorite monument.

This item features a miniature model of the dome monument with a tiny patrol helicopter spinning around it, and a music box version of Rust's main theme song.

Page views: 5,748  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Rustige Egg - Blue

# Description __

An beautiful hand crafted white gold and sapphire encrusted egg, with a miniature monument contained inside.

This item features a miniature model of the lighthouse monument.

Page views: 4,289  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Salvaged Cleaver

# Description __

A powerful 2-handed melee weapon with high damage.

Page views: 5,286

# Salvaged Sword

# Description __

A powerful melee weapon made from a filed-down wrench. Great durability, good damage.

Page views: 5,960  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# SAM Site

# Description __

A surface to air rocket site. Requires 25 electricity to function.

Page views: 56,010  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

A heavy hazmat suit made from radiation resistant rubber.

# Scrap

# Description __

A pile of random unidentified junk. Can be used in a research bench to get the blueprint of items you currently have. Alternatively, you can use it in the different workbenchs to unlock the blueprints of the corresponding tier.

Page views: 4,633  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/seed.corn~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/seed.corn~history)



# Corn Seed

# Description __

Corn seeds can be found when picking wild Corn plants. These seeds can be planted in the ground and grown to collect additional food.

Planting these seeds in a planter, and then watering them with large quantities of water yields significantly more Corn and faster groth.

Page views: 6,346  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Hemp Seed

# Description __

Hemp seeds can be found when picking wild Hemp. These seeds can be planted in the ground and grown to collect additional cloth.

Planting these seeds in a planter, and then watering them with large quantities of water yields significantly more cloth and faster groth.

Page views: 13,134  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/seed.pumpkin~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/seed.pumpkin~history)



# Pumpkin Seed

# Description __

Pumpkin Seeds can be found when picking wild Pumpkin plants. These seeds can be planted in the ground and grown to collect additional food.

Planting these seeds in a planter, and then watering them with large quantities of water yields significantly more Pumpkins and faster groth.

Page views: 3,874  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Boots

# Description __

Work boots.

# Stats __

Damage Type | Percentage  
---|---  
Projectile | 10 %  
Melee | 10 %  
Bite | 3 %  
Radiation | 3 %  
Cold | 8 %  
  
# Loot Rates __

Container | Chance  
---|---  
Locked Crate | 3 %  
Elite Tier Crate | 1 %  
Military Crate | 1 %  
Oil Rig Scientist | 0.1 %  
Heavy Scientist | 0.1 %  
  
Item does not stack and its despawn time is 20 min.

Page views: 3,171  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/shotgun.double~history)



# Double Barrel Shotgun

# Description __

A Shotgun with two barrels allowing two shots to be fired in quick succession before needing to reload. Deals devastating damage at close ranges.

Page views: 7,163  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Pump Shotgun](/rust/item/shotgun.pump)

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/shotgun.pump~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/shotgun.pump~history)



# Pump Shotgun

# Description __

A shotgun that holds six rounds and deals devastating damage up close.

# Pump Shotgun __

* * *

The Pump Shotgun is a reliable and powerful close-range weapon in Rust. With a capacity of 6 shells, it can quickly take down enemies at close range.

The Pump Shotgun is a craftable weapon in Rust. It requires the following materials to craft:

Item | Quantity  
---|---  
Metal Pipe | 2  
Gears | 2  
Spring | 1  
High Quality Metal | 5  
  
The Pump Shotgun is also sometimes found in various loot containers such as barrels, crates, and boxes.

## Attachment Compatibility __

* * *

The Pump Shotgun is compatible with the following attachments:

  * Muzzle: 
    * Muzzle Boost
    * Silencer
  * Sight: 
    * 8x Zoom Scope
    * Holo Sight
    * Simple Handmade Sight
    * Laser Sight
  * Magazine: 
    * 12 Gauge Slug



## Damage __

* * *

The Pump Shotgun deals 10 damage per pellet and has a capacity of 6 shells. Each shot can fire up to 12 pellets.

## Interesting Facts __

* * *

  * The Pump Shotgun was added to Rust in the November 2014 update.
  * The Pump Shotgun is based on the real-life Remington 870 shotgun.
  * The Pump Shotgun is a popular weapon among players due to its versatility and effectiveness in close-range combat.

# Spas-12 Shotgun

# Description __

A semi automatic military issue shotgun that shreds enemies at close ranges.

Page views: 7,397  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Waterpipe Shotgun

# Description __

A Shotgun. Fires a single round before reloading.

Page views: 6,153  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Metal horizontal embrasure

# Description __

Static shutter that form a metal horizontal embrasure over your window frame.

Page views: 3,273  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Metal Vertical embrasure

# Description __

Static shutter that form a metal vertical embrasure over your window frame.

Page views: 4,110  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
